<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Pharmaceutical_sector">Pharmaceutical sector</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Risk_management&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Pharmaceutical sector"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p>The principles and tools for quality risk management are increasingly being applied to different aspects of pharmaceutical quality systems. These aspects include development, manufacturing, distribution, inspection, and submission/review processes throughout the lifecycle of drug substances, drug products, biological and biotechnological products (including the use of raw materials, solvents, excipients, packaging and labeling materials in drug products, biological and biotechnological products). Risk management is also applied to the assessment of microbiological contamination in relation to pharmaceutical products and cleanroom manufacturing environments.<sup id="cite&#95;ref-Sandle&#95;63-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Sandle-63"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>63<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Supply_chain">Supply chain</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Risk_management&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Supply chain"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1320445320" /><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Supply_chain_risk_management" title="Supply chain risk management">Supply chain risk management</a></div>
<p>Supply chain risk management (SCRM) aims at maintaining <a href="/wiki/Supply_chain" title="Supply chain">supply chain</a> continuity in the event of scenarios or incidents which could interrupt normal business and hence profitability. Risks to the supply chain range from everyday to exceptional, including unpredictable natural events (such as <a href="/wiki/Tsunami" title="Tsunami">tsunamis</a> and <a href="/wiki/Pandemic" title="Pandemic">pandemics</a>) to counterfeit products, and reach across quality, security, to resiliency and product integrity. Mitigation of these risks can involve various elements of the business including <a href="/wiki/Logistics" title="Logistics">logistics</a> and cybersecurity, as well as the areas of finance and operations.
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Travel">Travel</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Risk_management&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Travel"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p>Travel risk management is concerned with how organisations assess the risks to their <a href="/wiki/Business_travel" title="Business travel">staff when travelling</a>, especially when travelling overseas. In the field of <a href="/wiki/International_standard" title="International standard">international standards</a>, ISO 31030:2021 addresses good practice in travel risk management.<sup id="cite&#95;ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>64<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>
</p><p>The Global Business Travel Association's education and research arm, the GBTA Foundation. found in 2015 that most businesses covered by their research employed travel risk management protocols aimed at ensuring the safety and well-being of their business travelers.<sup id="cite&#95;ref-gbtaf&#95;65-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-gbtaf-65"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>65<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Six key principles of travel risk awareness put forward by the association are preparation, awareness of surroundings and people, keeping a low profile, adopting an unpredictable routine, communications and layers of protection.<sup id="cite&#95;ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>66<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Traveler tracking using mobile tracking and messaging technologies had by 2015 become a widely used aspect of travel risk management.<sup id="cite&#95;ref-gbtaf&#95;65-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-gbtaf-65"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>65<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Risk_communication">Risk communication</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Risk_management&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Risk communication"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<div class="excerpt-block"><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1066933788">.mw-parser-output .excerpt-hat .mw-editsection-like{font-style:normal}</style><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1320445320" /><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable dablink excerpt-hat selfref">This section is an excerpt from <a href="/wiki/Risk_communication" title="Risk communication">Risk communication</a>.<span class="mw-editsection-like plainlinks"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Risk_communication&amp;action=edit">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div><div class="excerpt">
<p><a href="/wiki/Risk_communication" title="Risk communication">Risk communication</a> is a complex cross-disciplinary academic field that is part of risk management and related to fields like <a href="/wiki/Crisis_communication" title="Crisis communication">crisis communication</a>. The goal is to make sure that targeted audiences understand how risks affect them or their communities by appealing to their values.<sup id="cite&#95;ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>67<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite&#95;ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>68<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>
</p><p>Risk communication is particularly important in <a href="/wiki/Disaster_preparedness" class="mw-redirect" title="Disaster preparedness">disaster preparedness</a>,<sup id="cite&#95;ref-Risk&#95;communication&#95;:0&#95;69-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Risk_communication_:0-69"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>69<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Public_health" title="Public health">public health</a>,<sup id="cite&#95;ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>70<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> and preparation for major <a href="/wiki/Global_catastrophic_risk" title="Global catastrophic risk">global catastrophic risk</a>.<sup id="cite&#95;ref-Risk&#95;communication&#95;:0&#95;69-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Risk_communication_:0-69"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>69<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> For example, the <a href="/wiki/Effects_of_climate_change" title="Effects of climate change">impacts of climate change</a> and <a href="/wiki/Climate_risk" title="Climate risk">climate risk</a> effect every part of society, so communicating that risk is an important <a href="/wiki/Climate_communication" title="Climate communication">climate communication</a> practice, in order for societies to plan for <a href="/wiki/Climate_change_adaptation" title="Climate change adaptation">climate adaptation</a>.<sup id="cite&#95;ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>71<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Similarly, in <a href="/wiki/Pandemic_prevention" title="Pandemic prevention">pandemic prevention</a>, <a href="/wiki/Risk_perception" title="Risk perception">understanding of risk</a> helps communities stop the spread of disease and improve responses.<sup id="cite&#95;ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>72<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>
</p><p>Risk communication deals with possible risks and aims to raise awareness of those risks to encourage or persuade changes in behavior to relieve threats in the long term. On the other hand, crisis communication is aimed at raising awareness of a specific type of threat, the magnitude, outcomes, and specific behaviors to adopt to reduce the threat.<sup id="cite&#95;ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>73<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>
</p><p>Risk communication in <a href="/wiki/Food_safety" title="Food safety">food safety</a> is part of the <a href="/wiki/Food_safety_risk_analysis" class="mw-redirect" title="Food safety risk analysis">risk analysis framework</a>. Together with risk assessment and risk management, risk communication aims to reduce <a href="/wiki/Foodborne_illness" title="Foodborne illness">foodborne illnesses</a>. Food safety risk communication is an obligatory activity for food safety authorities<sup id="cite&#95;ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>74<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> in countries, which adopted the <a href="/wiki/Agreement_on_the_Application_of_Sanitary_and_Phytosanitary_Measures" title="Agreement on the Application of Sanitary and Phytosanitary Measures">Agreement on the Application of Sanitary and Phytosanitary Measures</a>.
</p><p>Risk communication also exists on a smaller scale. For instance, the risks associated with personal medical decisions have to be communicated to that individual along with their family.<sup id="cite&#95;ref-Risk&#95;communication&#95;:12&#95;75-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Risk_communication_:12-75"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>75<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>
</p>
</div></div>
